If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

If you do not receive your duplicate notice by February 4, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

On January 5, 2023, we sent a request for initial evidence for your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290146896. The request for evidence explains what we need from you. We will not take action on your case until we receive the evidence or the deadline to submit it expires. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
